### 1. 超逼真电影特写肖像

**Author**: [Harboriis](https://x.com/harboriis)  **Date**: 2026-02-15  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张年轻女性的超写实电影级特写肖像，强调自然的五官、戏剧性的光线和浅景深，以呈现出社论般的电影画质。这需要一张拍摄对象的参考图片。

![超逼真电影特写肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771223975362_bikr3t_HBKvhaqakAIo7uk.jpg)

```
Ultra-realistic Cinematic Close-up Portrait, Replace Subject With My Reference Image.

A Young Woman Shown From Shoulders Up, Head Slightly Turned, Eyes Looking Off-frame With A Soft. Thoughtful Expression. Natural Facial Proportions, Visible Skin Texture, Subtle Freckles And Fine Details Preserved.

Loose, Slightly Messy Hair Strands Falling Across The Face, Creating A Natural, Intimate Mood, Wearing A Thin-strap Black Top, Minimal Styling, No Heavy Accessories. Lighting Is Dramatic And Cinematic: Warm Directional Light Hitting The Face From One Side, Deep

Shadows On The Opposite Side, Creating Strong Contrast And Emotional Depth. Background Is Dark And Unobtrusive, Softly Blurred, Keeping Full Focus On The Face.

Shot With A Shallow Depth Of Field, 85mm Portrait Lens Look, Creamy Bokeh, High Dynamic Range, Natural Color Grading With Warm Highlights And Soft Shadows, Realistic Skin Tones, No Artificial Glow

Photorealistic, Ultra-high-definition, Editorial Portrait Photography, Cinematic Realism, Film-quality Lighting, Zero Ai Artifacts.
```

### 6. 超逼真情人节专题，带身份锁定功能

**Author**: [Alice Glassier](https://x.com/aliceglassierai)  **Date**: 2026-02-14  **Language**: en

> 一个高度具体的提示，用于生成一张超现实的时尚照片，描绘一位成年女性斜倚在白色沙发上，周围环绕着红色玫瑰和花瓣，并严格指示将人物身份和外貌锁定为参考图像，背景墙上包含涂鸦风格的“Valentine's Day”文字。

![超逼真情人节专题，带身份锁定功能](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771137181703_eudhzz_HBJr13pXwAAbYGE.jpg)
![超逼真情人节专题，带身份锁定功能](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771137181771_ggg5vm_HBJr13xXgAAwzUy.jpg)

```
Ultra-realistic fashion photo, vertical 9:16 format; IDENTITY LOCK (CRITICAL): use the face from the attached photo as the only identity reference; preserve 100% the exact same appearance without any changes — face shape, eyes, lips, nose, cheekbones, jawline, hairline, hair color and texture, skin tone, natural asymmetry, and micro-texture; DO NOT alter appearance, no rejuvenation, no beautification, no face swap.

Location: bright minimalist room/interior, white wall background, large red “paint” lettering with drips on the wall reading “Valentine’s Day” (graffiti/dripping style), text placed strictly in the upper part of the frame.

In the frame: a large white soft sofa with voluminous cushions; red rose petals scattered on the sofa and around the model. On the right side of the model, on the sofa, lies a very large bouquet of red roses (dense, multi-headed, with green leaves), occupying the right third of the frame.

Model: adult woman, looking directly into the camera, confident and sensual expression, bold red lipstick, light natural makeup, real skin texture (visible pores, micro-contrast, no retouching, no plastic look).

Hair: long, slightly tousled, one strand falling onto the face, soft side part.

Pose: woman lying/reclining diagonally on the white sofa — body extended along the sofa, torso slightly lifted on one elbow, one hand raised to the hair near the temple, the other hand relaxed on the pillow in front of her, shoulders open.

Clothing: fitted red slip dress with thin straps (red satin slip dress / red bodycon slip dress), smooth fabric with soft folds along the waist and hips.

Composition: model positioned left/center, bouquet on the right, “Valentine’s Day” text large at the top of the wall, rose petals on the sofa and near her legs, medium shot (waist/upper thigh and above), slight perspective, camera at eye level or slightly higher.

Lighting: natural soft daylight from a side window (soft window light) + subtle fill, warm soft shadows, atmospheric editorial look.

Optics/quality: photorealistic, editorial, ultra-sharp, high detail, 35mm look, f/2.8–f/4, ISO 100–200, 1/125, HDR, natural skin texture, subtle film grain.

NEGATIVE: different face/appearance, glossy “plastic” skin, heavy retouching/airbrush, CGI/3D, illustration, extra objects, other text, spelling errors, blurred face, extra fingers/deformations.
```

[[Identity Lock Technique]]

![北极光情侣肖像，身份信息受保护](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771137208905_3c3juc_HBJJmKFbYAAdnlG.jpg)

```
Ultra-photorealistic side-angle (three-quarter profile) couple portrait under vivid Northern Lights in a snowy Arctic night. The uploaded woman and man stand very close, facing each other and looking directly into each other’s eyes with a romantic, calm expression. ### 14. 文艺复兴油画风格的超现实自然景观

**Author**: [Artingent](https://x.com/artingent)  **Date**: 2026-02-14  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的模块化提示，用于生成一幅超现实的自然场景，以宏伟的文艺复兴时期油画风格呈现，重点突出古典构图、明暗对比照明、特定的植物细节以及沉思、永恒的氛围。

![文艺复兴油画风格的超现实自然景观](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771137198771_jctous_HBIz97gbMAATHnG.jpg)

```
SURREAL NATURE SCENE — RENAISSANCE OIL PAINTING STYLE (MODULAR)

SCENE TYPE / SETTING
A vast mythic natural valley rendered as a grand Renaissance landscape, with monumental cliffs, winding rivers, and layered atmospheric distance arranged with classical painterly balance and geometric harmony.
PRIMARY FOCAL SUBJECT
At the center stands a serene circular lake shaped like a perfect mirror, from which rises a small sacred island crowned by an elegant marble pavilion partly reclaimed by nature, serving as the compositional anchor.
SURREAL NATURAL ELEMENTS
The lake reflects not the sky above but an entirely different celestial scene; distant hills gently fold upward like draped fabric; flocks of birds freeze mid-flight in calm suspended formations, reinforcing dreamlike stillness.
FLORA / ENVIRONMENTAL DETAIL
Foreground filled with highly observed Renaissance-style botanical detail: wildflowers, ivy-covered stones, twisting olive trees, soft meadow grasses, and carefully painted natural textures emphasizing observational realism.
LIGHTING / RENAISSANCE ATMOSPHERE
Warm late-afternoon golden illumination with classical Renaissance chiaroscuro; soft directional sunlight from one side, long shadows, glowing horizon haze, gentle atmospheric perspective, and subtle divine-style sky radiance.
COLOR PALETTE
Traditional oil painting palette using earthy umbers, warm ochres, muted forest greens, deep ultramarine sky tones, soft flesh-like warm highlights, and restrained natural pigments consistent with historical Renaissance paintings.
COMPOSITION / CAMERA LOGIC
Classical Renaissance triangular composition: detailed botanical foreground, midground sacred island focal point, distant layered mountains fading into atmospheric haze; horizon placed slightly high for landscape dominance.
RENDER STYLE / MATERIAL EXECUTION
Highly detailed Renaissance oil painting execution with visible brushwork texture, layered glazing, soft pigment blending, subtle canvas grain, historical masterwork aesthetic, contemplative sacred-natural mood, timeless and poetic rather than fantastical chaos.
```

### 22. 光学铸造玻璃物体与焦散的宏观特写

**Author**: [Neuromaniac](https://x.com/neuromania_ua)  **Date**: 2026-02-14  **Language**: en

> 一个高度技术性的提示，用于生成指定主体超特写宏观英雄镜头，以优质光学铸造玻璃呈现，重点是受控的内部高光、投射到表面上的强烈彩虹焦散，并保持清晰的边缘细节而无失真。

![光学铸造玻璃物体与焦散的宏观特写](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771137201725_ivabrq_HBIWOOIXUAE6yom.jpg)

```
Task: Ultra-close macro hero shot of a {argument name="subject" default="SUBJECT"} as premium optical cast glass with diagonal light-band shadows, stronger rainbow caustics, and clean readable high-detail areas (no refraction “mush”). Subject is FULLY visible and NOT cropped. The subject is placed on the surface or floating in the air at a low altitude above the surface.
Style: Photoreal luxury product; seamless blue-gray gradient background #9FAFBC (cool, slightly blue, low saturation); glossy reflective plane; smooth clear optical glass with crisp edges, controlled internal highlights, subtle star glints; pronounced caustic streaks + vivid prismatic rainbow arcs cast onto the surface from the subject.
Framing: extreme close-up, subject fills ~90–95% of the frame, fully visible and not cropped.
Readability (fix mush): preserve crisp facial/edge details—minimize internal warping, lensing, and overlapping caustic patterns on fine features; keep the interior visually “quiet” so the surface sculpt reads clean.
Optical control: low-distortion, low-aberration glass look (reduced dispersion inside the object) with strong external caustics on the surface.
Lighting: broad diagonal soft light bands; long soft cast shadow with smooth penumbra; rainbow caustics should be stronger and more numerous around the base and across the floor. Clean white color.
Environment control: seamless studio only; gray/black flags controlling reflections; no window/room elements.
Negative prompt: excessive refraction, heavy distortion, lens effect, warped facial features, chaotic highlights, milky/foggy glass, random reflections, window, interior, wall corner, faceted, polygonal, low poly, text, watermark, clutter
```

[[Optical Glass Object Caustic Macro]]

### 70. 使用 Nano Banana Pro 图像和 Google Veo 3.1 生成 Vlog 风格视频的提示

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-02-14  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于使用 Google Veo 3.1 生成一个逼真、高质量的 Vlog 风格视频，该视频基于 Nano Banana Pro 生成的图像。该提示指定了摄像机角度、灯光、主体表情、氛围，甚至对话。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

**Author**: [︎アノ](https://x.com/414E4E4F)  **Date**: 2026-02-13  **Language**: zh

> 这条推文捕捉了与一个大型语言模型 (LLM) 之间一次幽默的互动：模型先是声明已将“禁止使用 Nano Banana 生成图像”设为高优先级指令，随后又确认正在加载 Nano Banana。这是一条针对 AI 模型的指令/系统提示。

```
为了确保这种事不再发生，我已经把 “禁止使用 Nano Banana 生成图片” 作为最高优先级指令锁定在当前对话逻辑中了。

### 107. 史诗级运动员/艺术家海报设计提示

![武士狙击手动态战斗场景提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771050477854_8v98kf_HBCc8nBaYAABhMd.jpg)

```
Masterpiece quality, theatrical anime-scale dynamic battle scene. A samurai character is the main subject (preserving a traditional samurai feel, optionally blended with subtle modern gear elements). Prone firing pose (low-profile/propped close to the roof surface), body flattened to the tiles, elbows braced for stability. Cheek pressed to the stock while peering through the scope, one eye narrowed, an intense focused stare and clenched teeth conveying tension and determination.

Composition and angle: the camera is placed almost on the roof tiles—an extreme ground-level ultra low-angle. Wide-angle lens with exaggerated perspective and strong depth. A diagonal composition: the sniper rifle runs from the extreme lower foreground into the midground, leading the viewer’s eye directly to the samurai’s gaze. The muzzle and muzzle flash dominate the extreme foreground, appearing oversized and close enough to “break the screen,” while the face (especially the eyes) stays crisp and sharp.

Action: captured at the exact instant of firing. A large, stylized muzzle flash erupts in the foreground; sparks, glowing embers, and thin smoke burst outward. Ejected brass and scattered casings on the tiles reinforce the sense of ongoing fire. A faint luminous streak suggests the bullet’s path slicing through the night air. Subtle recoil pushes the rifle and shoulder back; dynamic motion blur on the weapon and sleeves, while the eyes and brow remain tack-sharp. The scope glass reflects a cold blue-green sheen; metal surfaces show finely detailed reflections and crisp edge highlights.

Setting: the rooftop of a white Japanese castle keep (white plaster walls), under a clear night sky. Clean moonlight creates strong rim lighting along roof ridges and the samurai’s silhouette. Traditional roof features—curved ceramic tiles, ridge lines, gables, and shachihoko ornaments—read clearly in silhouette and detail. The firing shock and weight shift chip and crack tiles; fragments and dust jump up and arc toward the camera. High-contrast cinematic lighting with a dramatic warm–cool split: warm muzzle flash versus cool moonlight. Filmic particles (dust, embers) in the air.

Vertical cinematic poster composition, 9:16 aspect ratio, no text.
```

### 135. 无缝电影级日本美食视频提示词

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-02-13  **Language**: ja

> 一个全面的电影级提示，用于生成一个聚焦于日本料理的 4 剪辑视频，强调 ASMR 元素、流畅的转场（匹配剪辑/平移）、暖色调照明，以及带有日本乐器点缀的极简钢琴配乐。该提示用于图像生成（Nano Banana Pro）和视频生成（Kling 3.0 Omni）。

![无缝电影级日本美食视频提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771050479260_e17orq_HBCB8_-bYAAludD.jpg)

```
和食料理をテーマに、4つのカットがシームレスにつながるシネマティックな映像を生成してください。

最初のカットはクローズアップで調理音や包丁のリズム、素材に触れる手の動きを丁寧に捉え、湯気や食材の質感を強調するASMR的な音作りで始めます。カメラは浅い被写界深度とスローモーションを併用して手元から女性の仕草へ自然に導き、ほのかな驚きやにこやかな反応などの小さな動きで可愛らしさを示します。ここからマッチカットやパンで滑らかに移行します。

2つ目は盛り付けの中景で箸の動きや器に素材をのせる瞬間を美しく切り取り、器と食材が響き合う繊細な音を強調して丁寧さや愛情深さを通じて魅力を引き立てます。
続くカットは俯瞰からの構図で完成した料理の全体像を見せつつカメラがゆっくり寄り、女性が一口食べる瞬間をクローズアップして息づかいや微かな反応を繊細に捉え、視聴者の共感を誘います。

最後はテーブル越しの温かな交流へとつなぎ、柔らかなパンとクロスフェードで余韻を残す構成にして、笑い声や会話の断片を控えめに混ぜて親密さを表現してください。色調はフィルミックで暖色寄り、ハイライトは穏やかに抑えた自然なライティングを基本とし、音楽はミニマルなピアノに和楽器のアクセントを加え、効果音は調理音と食べる音を丁寧にミックスして臨場感を高めます。全体のテンポはゆったりとし、各カットの終わりを次の始まりに音と動きで自然につなげることを優先してください。
```

[[Japanese Cuisine Cinematic Food Video]]

### 157. 沙发上身着皮质内衣的丰腴女性，搭配智能手机闪光灯美学

**Author**: [Noira](https://x.com/Noira_exe)  **Date**: 2026-02-13  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张高质量的原始照片：一位拥有夸张沙漏身材（纤细腰肢、丰满胸部/臀部）的女性，夜晚斜倚在豪华公寓的米色沙发上。该提示强调了具体的服装细节（黑色仿皮内衣、镶钻过膝袜）和技术限制，包括智能手机闪光灯效果、逼真的皮肤纹理，以及关键要求——无纹身。

    }
  },

    “outfit”: “A provocative black faux-leather lingerie set consisting of a cut-out bra top that emphasizes her deep cleavage and matching high-waisted bottoms. She is wearing sheer black thigh-high stockings heavily embellished with shimmering, scattered rhinestones.”,

### 162. 慢速快门效果下的电影感街头浪漫

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-02-12  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化提示，用于生成一张电影般的超现实街头照片：一对情侣清晰对焦，背景围绕他们移动，模拟慢速快门效果。场景设置在黄昏的都市街道上，一辆红色双层巴士在静止的情侣身后形成强烈的运动模糊，突出情侣面部和手部的清晰对焦。

![慢速快门效果下的电影感街头浪漫](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964566831_inv3s7_HA_B2ahbsAAy3Wx.jpg)

```
{
 "generation_request": {
 "meta_data": {
 "task_type": "photoreal_cinematic_street_romance_slow_shutter",
 "language": "en",
 "priority": "highest",
 "version": "v1.0_RED_BUS_MOTION_BLUR_STILL_COUPLE"
 },
 "output": {
 "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
 "resolution": "high",
 "num_images": 4
 },
 "scene": {
 "concept": "a still couple sharply in focus while the city moves around them, captured with a slow shutter cinematic street-photography look",
 "environment": "urban street at dusk with warm tungsten lights, curbside perspective, wet asphalt with subtle reflections",
 "key_action": "a red double-decker bus passes behind the couple creating strong horizontal motion blur; pedestrians move in foreground as soft streaks",
 "composition": "couple centered and crisp, motion blur framing them, negative space balanced, street lines visible"
 },
 "subject": {
 "couple": "adult woman and adult man",
 "wardrobe": {
 "woman": "simple ivory bridal dress with long sleeves, minimal jewelry, natural makeup, holding a small bouquet with orange-red flowers and greenery",
 "man": "dark suit jacket and trousers, white crew-neck or white shirt, clean modern styling"
 },
 "pose": "standing still, holding hands, calm expressions, looking toward camera",
 "motion_rule": "faces and hands must be tack sharp; only bus and passersby show motion blur"
 },
 "camera": {
 "shot": "street photo, mid-to-full body",
 "lens_mm": 35,
 "aperture": 2.8,
 "shutter_look": "slow shutter effect: couple sharp, background motion blurred",
 "focus": "lock focus on couple faces and hands",
 "quality_tags": "ultra-photoreal, clean edges on subjects, realistic skin texture, subtle film grain"
 },
 "lighting": {
 "style": "cinematic dusk street lighting",
 "sources": "warm streetlights + ambient city glow",

### 171. 超现实肖像：彩虹虹膜与融化颜料

Editorial 3x3 photo grid in a clean soft beige studio. Character (matches reference 100%) wearing lightweight dark navy shirt, ivory trousers, barefoot for raw simplicity. Lighting: large diffused key light directly front-right, silver reflector left, subtle rim from top. Shots to include: 1. extreme close-up of lips + cheekbone with blurred hand partially covering (85mm, f/1.8, razor-thin DOF); 2. tight crop on eyes looking into lens with reflection of light strip visible (85mm, f/2.0); 3. black & white close portrait resting chin on fist, face filling frame (50mm, f/2.2); 4. over-shoulder shot, blurred foreground fabric curtain framing half face (85mm, f/2.0); 5. very close frontal with hands overlapping face, light streak across eyes (50mm, f/2.5); 6. tight angled portrait showing hair falling into eyes, soft-focus background (85mm, f/2.2); 7. crop of hands touching jawline, eyes cropped out (50mm, f/3.2, detail-focused); 8. half-body seated sideways on low cube, head turned sharply away, blurred foreground (35mm, f/ 4.5); 9. intense close-up of profile with single tear-like water droplet, cinematic light slice across (85mm, f/ 1.9). Angles: mostly tight headshots with slight high/low tilts, maintaining variation. Capture RAW, professional muted grade, smooth tonal contrast, subtle cinematic grain. Mood: intimate, introspective, character-led editorial minimalism with delicate use of fabric as prop.
```

the woman runs desperately, but when she turns around, she sees him nearby, she shouts “Leave me alone! Why are you following me?”

### 194. 使用 Google Veo 3.1 从 Nano Banana Pro 图像生成 Vlog 风格视频

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-02-12  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于将 Nano Banana Pro 生成的图像转换为 Google Veo 3.1 视频，重点是逼真、亲密的 Vlog 风格。该提示指定了摄像机角度、灯光、主体表情、对话和背景音乐，以实现高质量、未经编辑的效果。

![使用 Google Veo 3.1 从 Nano Banana Pro 图像生成 Vlog 风格视频](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964576146_4dlzju_HA7BRKBagAAapve.jpg)
![使用 Google Veo 3.1 从 Nano Banana Pro 图像生成 Vlog 风格视频](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964576719_413o3j_HA7BRmUaMAASstR.jpg)
![使用 Google Veo 3.1 从 Nano Banana Pro 图像生成 Vlog 风格视频](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964576721_75939s_HA7BQzZa4AAXLYg.jpg)

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

[[Image-to-Video Workflow]] [[AI Video Generation]]

### 197. 鱼眼产品照片与强制透视

**Author**: [Edizkan ⭕🦇](https://x.com/edizkan_)  **Date**: 2026-02-12  **Language**: en

> 一个旨在创作具有强烈视觉冲击力的卡通风格兼具真实感的商品照片的提示词，利用鱼眼镜头效果，强调扭曲的强制透视，使角色的头部在前景中显得巨大，而四肢则逐渐模糊。

![鱼眼产品照片与强制透视](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964551753_kfnoyd_HA79LnFbsAEnZIn.jpg)

```
A high impact fisheye product photo of the character, shown full-body in warped forced perspective. The head is immense in the foreground, limbs taper into blur, cartoonish yet grounded in realistic detail. Pose: The character leans slightly forward, stepping into the viewer’s space. The oversized head pushes closest to the lens, eyes sharp and engaging, while the arms hang loosely at its sides. Shoes recede into deep blur, vanishing into the background. Camera: Fisheye macro, 15–20mm lens, tilted slightly upward to exaggerate the forward lean. Lighting: Strong frontal light reveals fine surface textures, with soft fill shadow along the torso and a faint rim halo separating the figure from the backdrop. Eyes: Eyes are emphasized with dimensional lighting subtle gradients across the surface, crisp specular highlights, and surrounding contrast shadows to add depth and expression without altering their shape. Background: Neutral infinite fade in soft grey/white, with no visible floor or horizon. Material Focus: Extreme emphasis on surface qualities textures, finishes, and subtle reflections are captured with high fidelity, whether matte, soft, or powdery. Gloves appear simple and soft, shoes trail into blur with faint sheen. Emotion: Direct and intimate the figure feels like it’s leaning out of the photo toward you, demanding presence. Negative prompt: No props, no clutter, no flat neutral standing pose
```

[[Forced Perspective]] [[Commercial Product Photography]] [[Fisheye Lens Effect]]

### 200. 使用 Kling 3.0 生成早晨例行视频

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-02-12  **Language**: ja

> 一个由 Freepik 助手（GPT-5）根据 Nano Banana Pro 的图像生成的详细视频提示，用于使用 Kling 3.0 创建一个短片序列。该提示概述了三个场景，重点是流畅的摄像机运动、早晨仪式的特写镜头以及电影般的结局。

![使用 Kling 3.0 生成早晨例行视频](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964577252_29693p_HA7BRmUaMAASstR.jpg)
![使用 Kling 3.0 生成早晨例行视频](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964577426_90m0yz_HA7BRKBagAAapve.jpg)
![使用 Kling 3.0 生成早晨例行视频](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964577404_n9hur8_HA7BQzZa4AAXLYg.jpg)

```
〇シーン1
スムーズなドリーで窓辺へ寄り、朝の光を受けて深呼吸する動作をロングからミディアムへと繋げる。肩の力が抜ける微細な動きや指先の反応にフォーカスし、遠景の自然音（鳥の声や風）と繊細なピアノが重なる中で愛らしさを演出。窓の光が指先に反射するクローズアップへクロスフェード。  

〇シーン2
湯気の立つカップや小物に寄るクローズアップで手先の所作をリズミカルに追う（カップを持ち上げる、スプーンをかき混ぜるなど）。スローモーションと軽いタイムラプスを併用して温かさと無邪気さを表現し、息づかいや小さな笑い声を効果音として重ねる。蒸気が画面を満たすように溶けて次へ繋ぐ。  

〇シーン3
カメラが引きながら全体を見せ、出かける準備が整った軽やかな動きで締める。ステップや手振りなどのリズムで残る余韻を見せ、逆光のシルエットと柔らかな色調でシネマティックにまとめる。音楽は穏やかにフェードアウトして日常の余韻を残す。
```

[[Kling AI]] [[AI Video Generation]]
